# Serialization Performance Benchmark Report

## Abstract

Benchmark comparison of 4 serialization frameworks: Bebop, Msgpack, Protobuf, Simdjson.

## Experimental Setup

### Hardware Configuration

| Parameter | Value |
|-----------|-------|
| Machine | Mac Studio (Apple M3 Ultra) |
| Host | Andrews-Mac-Studio.local |
| CPU Count | 28 |
| MHz per CPU | 24 |
| CPU Scaling | Disabled |
| Build Type | release |
| Date | 2026-02-04T00:08:41+09:00 |
| Load Average | 3.20, 3.04, 2.64 |

### Cache Hierarchy

| Level | Type | Size |
|-------|------|------|
| L1 | Data | 64KB |
| L1 | Instruction | 128KB |
| L2 | Unified | 4096KB |

### Methodology

Each benchmark ran 10 times. Statistics: mean, median, stddev, CV. Throughput in bytes/second.

## Results

### Decode Performance

#### Bebop

## Conclusions

1. **Bebop Encode vs Msgpack**: Bebop faster in 15/19 (1.2x-19.4x). Best: OrderLarge (19.4x), OrderSmall (2.6x), TreeDeep (2.3x). Msgpack faster in 4/19. Losses: JsonSmall (1.40x slower), JsonLarge (1.16x slower), ChunkedText (1.10x slower), DocumentLarge (1.09x slower).

2. **Bebop Encode vs Protobuf**: Bebop faster in 22/22 (1.4x-12.6x). Best: OrderLarge (12.6x), ChunkedText (5.4x), LLMChunkLarge (5.3x). 

3. **Bebop Decode vs Msgpack**: Bebop faster in 18/19 (1.6x-129.5x). Best: OrderLarge (129.5x), Embedding1536 (22.5x), Embedding768 (21.6x). Msgpack faster in 1/19. Losses: JsonLarge (1.32x slower).

4. **Bebop Decode vs Protobuf**: Bebop faster in 19/19 (8.3x-212.2x). Best: TensorShardLarge (212.2x), OrderLarge (95.4x), EmbeddingBatch (44.2x). 

5. **Bebop Decode vs Simdjson Parse**: Bebop faster in 17/19 (1.2x-5741.0x). Best: TensorShardLarge (5741.0x), Embedding1536 (1674.9x), EmbeddingBatch (1078.8x). Simdjson faster in 2/19. Losses: JsonLarge (4.25x slower), JsonSmall (1.70x slower).

6. **Stability**: Mean CV across 149 benchmarks: 1.65%.

7. **Peak Throughput**:

   - Bebop Decode TensorShardLarge: 9.58 TB/s
   - Bebop Decode Embedding1536: 1.10 TB/s
   - Bebop Decode EmbeddingBatch: 964.13 GB/s
   - Bebop Decode EventLarge: 644.35 GB/s
   - Msgpack Decode TensorShardLarge: 608.60 GB/s
